<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('.new-nav ul .nav-search').click(function(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            var is_search = $(this).attr('data-icon');
            if (is_search=='show') {
                $(this).children('.fa').removeClass('fa-search');
                $(this).children('.fa').addClass('fa-times');
                $(this).attr('data-icon', 'hidden');
                $('#custom-search-input').show('fast');
            }else{
                $(this).children('.fa').removeClass('fa-times');
                $(this).children('.fa').addClass('fa-search');
                $(this).attr('data-icon', 'show');
                $('#custom-search-input').hide('slow');
            }
        });

        $(window).bind('scroll', function() {
            var navHeight = $( window ).height() - 100;
            if ($(window).scrollTop() > navHeight) {
                $('.new-nav').addClass('new-nav-fixed');
            }else{
                $('.new-nav').removeClass('new-nav-fixed');
            }
        });


        $('.new-nav .dropdown .print-nav-list li a').hover(function() {
            var get_page_id = $(this).attr('data-menu');
            $('.new-nav .dropdown .list-news .ajax-page').removeClass('active');
            $('.new-nav .dropdown .list-news #'+get_page_id).addClass('active');
        });

        $('.new-nav .nav-dropdown').hover(function() {
            $(".new-nav .nav-dropdown .dropdown").css('display', 'none');
            $(this).find('.dropdown').stop().fadeIn("slow");
            $(this).find('a i').addClass("down");
        }, function() {
            $(this).find('.dropdown').stop().fadeOut("fast");
            $(this).find('a i').removeClass("down");
        });
    });
</script> <div class="clearfix"></div>

<p>সম্পাদক : ইমদাদুল হক মিলন, ইস্ট ওয়েস্ট মিডিয়া গ্রুপ লিমিটেডের পক্ষে ময়নাল হোসেন চৌধুরী কর্তৃক প্রধান কার্যালয় : প্লট-৩৭১/এ, ব্লক-ডি, বসুন্ধরা, বারিধারা থেকে প্রকাশিত এবং প্লট-সি/৫২, ব্লক-কে, বসুন্ধরা, খিলক্ষেত, বাড্ডা, ঢাকা-১২২৯ ও সুপ্রভাত মিডিয়া লিমিটেড ৪ সিডিএ বাণিজ্যিক এলাকা, মোমিন রোড, চট্টগ্রাম-৪০০০ ও কালিবালা দ্বিতীয় বাইপাস রোড, বগুড়া থেকে মুদ্রিত। পিএবিএক্স : ০৯৬১২১২০০০০, ৮৪৩২৩৭২-৭৫, বার্তা বিভাগ ফ্যাক্স : ৮৪৩২৩৬৮-৬৯, বিজ্ঞাপন ফোন : ৮৪৩২০৪৮, বিজ্ঞাপন ফ্যাক্স : ৮৪৩২০৪৭, সার্কুলেশন : ৮৪৩২৩৭৬। <span class="eng_font">E-mail : <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="731a1d151c3318121f160118121d071b1c5d101c1e">[email&#160;protected]</a></p>

<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
        var body_width = $('body').width();
        if (body_width > 700) {
            $(".dropdown").hover(
                function() { $('.dropdown-menu', this).stop().fadeIn("fast");
                },
                function() { $('.dropdown-menu', this).stop().fadeOut("fast");
            });
        };
        $('.home-top-more-news li').hover(function() {
            $('.home-top-more-news ul li .more_news').stop().slideUp('slow');
            $(this).find('.more_news').stop().slideDown('slow');
        });

    function stripslashes(str) {
      return (str + '')
        .replace(/\\(.?)/g, function(s, n1) {
          switch (n1) {
            case '\\':
              return '\\';
            case '0':
              return '\u0000';
            case '':
              return '';
            default:
              return n1;
          }
        });
    }

    function social_btn_html(url) {
        return '<div class="socail_hover" style="height: 31px; bottom: -4px; right: 1px;">\
            <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https://www.kalerkantho.com/'+url+'" onclick="window.open(this.href, \'kalerkantho\',\
            \'left=20,top=20,width=700,height=500,toolbar=1,resizable=0\'); return false;"><i class="fa fa-facebook" aria-hidden="true"></i></a>\
            <a href="https://twitter.com/share?url=https://www.kalerkantho.com/'+url+'" onclick="window.open(this.href, \'kalerkantho\',\
            \'left=20,top=20,width=700,height=500,toolbar=1,resizable=0\'); return false;"><i class="fa fa-twitter" aria-hidden="true"></i></a>\
            <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=https://www.kalerkantho.com/'+url+'" onclick="window.open(this.href, \'kalerkantho\',\
            \'left=20,top=20,width=700,height=500,toolbar=1,resizable=0\'); return false;"><i class="fa fa-google-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></a>\
            </div>';
    }
    function ajax_fun(n_id,type=''){
        console.log('https://www.kalerkantho.com/home/print_cat/'+n_id+'/'+type);
        $('#ajax_news').html('');
        $.ajax({
            url: 'https://www.kalerkantho.com/home/print_cat/'+n_id+'/'+type,
        })
        .success(function(data) {
            // console.log(data);
            if(data.length){
                var json_obj = JSON.parse(data),
                // console.log(json_obj);
                output = '',
                a = 0;
            }else{return false;}

            var str = json_obj[0].n_date;
            var res = str.replace(/-/g , "/");
            var details1 = json_obj[0].n_details.substr(0, 90);
            var details =details1.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig, '');
            var newstype = 'print-edition';
            if (json_obj[0].m_type == 'feature') {
              newstype = "feature";
            }
            if (json_obj[0].main_image== null || json_obj[0].main_image=='') {
            var img = 'https://www.kalerkantho.com/assets/importent_images/common-thumbnails-img.jpg';
            }else{
            var img = 'https://www.kalerkantho.com/assets/news_images/'+res+'/thumbnails/'+json_obj[0].main_image;
            }
            var nUrl = newstype+'/'+json_obj[0].m_bangla+'/'+res+'/'+json_obj[0].n_id;

            output +='<div class="item col-sm-12 col-md-12" style="padding-right: 0;">';

                output +='<div class="col-sm-7 col-md-7 item-list">\
                    <div class="social_img">\
                        <img src="'+img+'" width="145" height="97" alt="...">\
                        '+social_btn_html(nUrl)+'\
                    </div>\
                    <a class="tab-news-title" href="'+newstype+'/'+json_obj[0].m_bangla+'/'+res+'/'+json_obj[0].n_id+'" title="">'+stripslashes(json_obj[0].n_head)+'</a>\
                    <p>'+details.trim()+'...</p>\
                </div>';

                output +='<div class="item col-sm-5 col-md-5 tab-news-list"><ul class="content mCustomScrollbar">';
                    for (var i in json_obj){
                        if (i==0) {
                            continue;
                        }
                        var newstype = 'print-edition';
                        if (json_obj[i].m_type == 'feature') {
                          newstype = "feature";
                        }
                        var str = json_obj[i].n_date;
                        var res = str.replace(/-/g , "/");
                        output +='<li><a href="'+newstype+'/'+json_obj[i].m_bangla+'/'+res+'/'+json_obj[i].n_id+'">'+stripslashes(json_obj[i].n_head)+'</a></li>';
                    }
                output +='</ul></div>';
            
            output +='</div>';

            $('#ajax_news').html(output);
            setTimeout(function(){
                $('#ajax_news').css('background',"none");
                $(".content").mCustomScrollbar();
            },500);
        });
    }
    // online_tab
    $('.online_tab .list li').click(function(event) {
        $('#ajax_news').css('background',"url('https://www.kalerkantho.com/assets/site/img/loading.gif') center 204px no-repeat");
        var n_id = $(this).attr('id');
        var type = $(this).attr('data-type');
        $('.online_tab .list li').removeClass('selected');
        $(this).addClass('selected');
        ajax_fun(n_id,type);
    });
    setTimeout(function(){
        ajax_fun('first-page');

    $('.home-print-tab-more-btn').click(function(event) {
        var is_display = $(this).attr('data-display');
        if (is_display=='hidden') {
            $(this).find('i').addClass('fa-angle-up').removeClass('fa-angle-down');
            $(this).attr('data-display','open');
            $('.online_tab ul').css('height', 'auto');
        }else{
            $(this).find('i').addClass('fa-angle-down').removeClass('fa-angle-up');
            $(this).attr('data-display','hidden');
            $('.online_tab ul').removeAttr("style");
        }
        return false;
    });

<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function($) {
    $('#pool_vote').click(function(event) {
        event.preventDefault();
        var ans_id = $('#pollResSum input:checked').val(),
            g_PoolType = $('[name="PoolType"]').val();
        $.ajax({
            url: 'https://www.kalerkantho.com/home/poll_vote',
            type: 'POST',
            data: {pollAnswer: ans_id, PoolType:g_PoolType},
        })
        .done(function(data) {
            // console.log(data);
            $('.progress_ans').html(data);
            $('.progress_area').hide();
            $('.progress_ans h4').show();
            setTimeout(function(){
                $('.progress_area').show('slow');
                $('.progress_ans h4').hide();
            },1000);
        });
        
    });
});
</script>

        });
    });

<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
    // fade in #back-top
    $(function () {
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(this).scrollTop() > 100) {
                $('#back-top').fadeIn();
            } else {
                $('#back-top').fadeOut();
            }
        });
        // scroll body to 0px on click
        $('#back-top a').click(function () {
            $('body,html').animate({
                scrollTop: 0
            }, 800);
            return false;
        });
    });
});
</script>

<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
    h = $('header').height()+50;
    $(".body-ad").stop().animate({top: h+"px"});
    $(window).scroll(function () {
        var st = $(this).scrollTop();
            // 269

        if (st == 0) {
            $(".body-ad").stop().animate({top: h+"px"});
        }else if(st <= h){
            $(".body-ad").stop().animate({top: "130px"});
        }else if(st < h){
            $(".body-ad").stop().animate({top: "10px"});
        }else{
            $(".body-ad").stop().animate({top: "10px"});
        };
    });
});
</script>

<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    $(window).scroll(function (event) {
        var scroll = $(window).scrollTop(),
            get_height = $('header').height();
            // console.log('rrrr '+get_height); 
        if (scroll > get_height) {
            
            // console.log(scroll+' rrrr '+get_height); 
            $('.new-nav').css({
                position: 'fixed',
                'z-index': '9999999',
                top: '0'
            });
        }else{
            $('.new-nav').css({
                position: 'static',
            });
        }
    });
});
</script>

<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
(function(){

function home_carousel_tab_news() {
    $('.carousel-showmanymoveone .item').each(function(){
        var itemToClone = $(this);
        for (var i=1;i<6;i++) {
            itemToClone = itemToClone.next();
            // wrap around if at end of item collection
            if (!itemToClone.length) {
                itemToClone = $(this).siblings(':first');
            }
            // grab item, clone, add marker class, add to collection
            itemToClone.children(':first-child').clone().addClass("cloneditem-"+(i)).appendTo($(this));
        }
    });
}
home_carousel_tab_news();

$('body').on('click', '.home-tab-news-lat-mos .nav li a', function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    home_carousel_tab_news();

});

}());
</script>
<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function() {
		$('.img-popup').click(function(event) {
			var main_img_src = $(this).find('img').attr('src'),
				close_btn = '<a href="#" class="close-img-popup"><i class="fa fa-times" aria-hidden="true"></i></a>',
				title = $(this).find('img').attr('alt'),
				caption = $(this).find('img').attr('data-caption'),
				img_src = '<img src="'+main_img_src+'">'+close_btn+'<h2>'+title+'</h2>';

			$('#img-popup-area').html('<div id="img-popup-inner-area">'+img_src+'</div>');
			$('#img-popup-area').fadeIn('slow');
		});
		$('body').on('click', '.close-img-popup', function(event) {
			event.preventDefault();
			$('#img-popup-area').fadeOut('400');
			$('#img-popup-area').html('');
		});
	});

<script type="6f20b65b8f17ef6ec0261031-text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('body').on('click', '.video-gallery-icon', function(event) {
            console.log('video-gallery-icon');
            $('#video-view').fadeIn('slow');
            var $this = $(this);
            var $iframe = $("<iframe>").attr("src", $this.data("link"));
            var $close = $('<a href="#" class="video-close"><i class="fa fa-times" aria-hidden="true"></i></a>');
            $("#video-view #iframe").html($close).append($iframe);
            $iframe.wrap("<div class='class-video'>");
            return false;
        });
        $('body').on('click', '#video-view .video-close', function(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            $('#video-view').fadeOut('slow');
            $('#video-view .class-video iframe').remove();
        });
    });
    </script>
